name: Comprehensive Travel Itinerary Planner

code: async def forward(self, taskInfo, extra_info):
    from collections import Counter
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []
    
    # Sub-task 1: Determine flight options
    reflexion_instruction_1 = "Sub-task 1: Determine the best flight options between cities, focusing on cost and time efficiency."
    cot_agent_1 = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'CoT Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_1 = LLMAgentBase(['feedback', 'correct'], 'Critic Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_1 = 3
    cot_inputs_1 = [taskInfo]
    thinking1, answer1 = await cot_agent_1(cot_inputs_1, extra_info, reflexion_instruction_1, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_1.id}, on the purpose of determining flight options, thinking: {thinking1.content}; answer: {answer1.content}")
    for i in range(N_max_1):
        feedback1, correct1 = await critic_agent_1([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1], extra_info, "Sub-task 1: Provide feedback on flight options. If correct, output 'True'.", i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_1.id}, on the purpose of reviewing flight options, feedback: {feedback1.content}; correct: {correct1.content}")
        if correct1.content == 'True':
            break
        cot_inputs_1.extend([thinking1, answer1, feedback1])
        thinking1, answer1 = await cot_agent_1(cot_inputs_1, extra_info, reflexion_instruction_1, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_1.id}, on the purpose of refining flight options, thinking: {thinking1.content}; answer: {answer1.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking1.content}; answer - {answer1.content}")

    # Sub-task 2: Determine self-driving options
    reflexion_instruction_2 = "Sub-task 2: Determine the best self-driving options between cities, focusing on cost and time efficiency."
    cot_agent_2 = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'CoT Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_2 = LLMAgentBase(['feedback', 'correct'], 'Critic Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_2 = 3
    cot_inputs_2 = [taskInfo]
    thinking2, answer2 = await cot_agent_2(cot_inputs_2, extra_info, reflexion_instruction_2, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_2.id}, on the purpose of determining self-driving options, thinking: {thinking2.content}; answer: {answer2.content}")
    for i in range(N_max_2):
        feedback2, correct2 = await critic_agent_2([taskInfo, thinking2, answer2], extra_info, "Sub-task 2: Provide feedback on self-driving options. If correct, output 'True'.", i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_2.id}, on the purpose of reviewing self-driving options, feedback: {feedback2.content}; correct: {correct2.content}")
        if correct2.content == 'True':
            break
        cot_inputs_2.extend([thinking2, answer2, feedback2])
        thinking2, answer2 = await cot_agent_2(cot_inputs_2, extra_info, reflexion_instruction_2, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_2.id}, on the purpose of refining self-driving options, thinking: {thinking2.content}; answer: {answer2.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2 output: thinking - {thinking2.content}; answer - {answer2.content}")

    # Sub-task 3: Select accommodations
    debate_instruction_3 = "Sub-task 3: Select suitable accommodations in each city, considering price and availability."
    debate_agents_3 = [LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Debate Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(3)]
    all_thinking_3 = [[] for _ in range(2)]
    all_answer_3 = [[] for _ in range(2)]
    for r in range(2):
        for i, agent in enumerate(debate_agents_3):
            if r == 0:
                t, a = await agent([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1, thinking2, answer2], extra_info, debate_instruction_3, is_sub_task=True)
            else:
                input_infos = [taskInfo] + [all_thinking_3[r-1][i]] + all_thinking_3[r-1][:i] + all_thinking_3[r-1][i+1:]
                t, a = await agent(input_infos, extra_info, debate_instruction_3, is_sub_task=True)
            agents.append(f"Debate agent {agent.id}, round {r}, on the purpose of selecting accommodations, thinking: {t.content}; answer: {a.content}")
            all_thinking_3[r].append(t)
            all_answer_3[r].append(a)
    final_decision_agent_3 = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Final Decision Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking3, answer3 = await final_decision_agent_3([taskInfo] + all_thinking_3[-1] + all_answer_3[-1], extra_info, debate_instruction_3, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Final Decision agent, on the purpose of finalizing accommodations, thinking: {thinking3.content}; answer: {answer3.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 3 output: thinking - {thinking3.content}; answer - {answer3.content}")

    # Sub-task 4: Choose dining options
    cot_sc_instruction_4 = "Sub-task 4: Choose dining options for each meal in each city, ensuring variety and budget adherence."
    N_4 = 3
    cot_sc_agents_4 = [LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'CoT-SC Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N_4)]
    thinking_mapping_4 = {}
    answer_mapping_4 = {}
    possible_answers_4 = []
    for i in range(N_4):
        thinking, answer = await cot_sc_agents_4[i]([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1, thinking2, answer2, thinking3, answer3], extra_info, cot_sc_instruction_4, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_sc_agents_4[i].id}, on the purpose of choosing dining options, thinking: {thinking.content}; answer: {answer.content}")
        possible_answers_4.append(answer.content)
        thinking_mapping_4[answer.content] = thinking
        answer_mapping_4[answer.content] = answer
    answer4 = Counter(possible_answers_4).most_common(1)[0][0]
    thinking4 = thinking_mapping_4[answer4]
    answer4 = answer_mapping_4[answer4]
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 4 output: thinking - {thinking4.content}; answer - {answer4.content}")

    # Sub-task 5: Select attractions
    cot_sc_instruction_5 = "Sub-task 5: Select attractions in each city, ensuring a balance of cultural and entertainment options."
    N_5 = 3
    cot_sc_agents_5 = [LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'CoT-SC Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N_5)]
    thinking_mapping_5 = {}
    answer_mapping_5 = {}
    possible_answers_5 = []
    for i in range(N_5):
        thinking, answer = await cot_sc_agents_5[i]([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1, thinking2, answer2, thinking3, answer3, thinking4, answer4], extra_info, cot_sc_instruction_5, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_sc_agents_5[i].id}, on the purpose of selecting attractions, thinking: {thinking.content}; answer: {answer.content}")
        possible_answers_5.append(answer.content)
        thinking_mapping_5[answer.content] = thinking
        answer_mapping_5[answer.content] = answer
    answer5 = Counter(possible_answers_5).most_common(1)[0][0]
    thinking5 = thinking_mapping_5[answer5]
    answer5 = answer_mapping_5[answer5]
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 5 output: thinking - {thinking5.content}; answer - {answer5.content}")

    # Sub-task 6: Compile the day-by-day itinerary
    debate_instruction_6 = "Sub-task 6: Based on the outputs from sub-tasks 1, 2, 3, 4, and 5, compile a detailed 7-day travel itinerary. Ensure the final itinerary avoids the following incorrect plans: [list incorrect plans]."
    debate_agents_6 = [LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Debate Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(3)]
    all_thinking_6 = [[] for _ in range(2)]
    all_answer_6 = [[] for _ in range(2)]
    for r in range(2):
        for i, agent in enumerate(debate_agents_6):
            if r == 0:
                t, a = await agent([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1, thinking2, answer2, thinking3, answer3, thinking4, answer4, thinking5, answer5], extra_info, debate_instruction_6, is_sub_task=True)
            else:
                input_infos = [taskInfo] + [all_thinking_6[r-1][i]] + all_thinking_6[r-1][:i] + all_thinking_6[r-1][i+1:]
                t, a = await agent(input_infos, extra_info, debate_instruction_6, is_sub_task=True)
            agents.append(f"Debate agent {agent.id}, round {r}, on the purpose of compiling itinerary, thinking: {t.content}; answer: {a.content}")
            all_thinking_6[r].append(t)
            all_answer_6[r].append(a)
    final_decision_agent_6 = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Final Decision Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking6, answer6 = await final_decision_agent_6([taskInfo] + all_thinking_6[-1] + all_answer_6[-1], extra_info, debate_instruction_6, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Final Decision agent, on the purpose of finalizing itinerary, thinking: {thinking6.content}; answer: {answer6.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 6 output: thinking - {thinking6.content}; answer - {answer6.content}")

    final_answer = self.make_final_answer(thinking6, answer6, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer
